      .               // Returns the type of an expression as a monotype.
      .               //
      .               // NB (1): This is the PRE-ADJUSTMENT TYPE for the expression.  That is, in

      .               /// Creates a type context and call the closure with a `TyCtxt` reference

     23 ( 0.00%)      pub fn create_global_ctxt(
      .                   s: &'tcx Session,

      .                   arena: &'tcx WorkerLocal<Arena<'tcx>>,

      .               pub fn get_source_file(&self, filename: &FileName) -> Option<Lrc<SourceFile>> {

    9,447 ( 0.01%)      fn extend_with<E: ExtendWith<T>>(&mut self, n: usize, mut value: E) {
        .                   self.reserve(n);
        .           
        .                   unsafe {
      270 ( 0.00%)              let mut ptr = self.as_mut_ptr().add(self.len());
        .                       // Use SetLenOnDrop to work around bug where compiler
        .                       // might not realize the store through `ptr` through self.set_len()
        .                       // don't alias.

        .           
        .                       // Write all elements except the last one

        .                           ptr::write(ptr, value.next());

        .                           ptr::write(ptr, value.last());

        .                       }

      .               crate fn update_extern_crate(&self, new_extern_crate: ExternCrate) -> bool {
